<div id="review_2611912852" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2611912852" />
    <a title="Mr Siegal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67002092-mr-siegal"><img alt="Mr Siegal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598466203p2/67002092.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2611912852?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mr Siegal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mr Siegal" href="/user/show/67002092-mr-siegal">Mr Siegal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781908968470" href="/book/show/17453349-coin-locker-babies">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2611912852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15449806379598117627">A Missed Opportunity <br/><br/>When I read the overview of the book, I was gripped. The book seemed so promising, and I instantly bought it and started reading it. I was quite disappointed. Overall, the characters are thin, and there is no apparent depth in anything. In addition, the book is marked by a lot of violence in one place, and little violence in another, singling that the tone of the book is inconsistent throughout. I could not empathise with the plight of the characters, nor did I agree that pe</span>
  <span id="freeText15449806379598117627" style="display:none">A Missed Opportunity <br /><br />When I read the overview of the book, I was gripped. The book seemed so promising, and I instantly bought it and started reading it. I was quite disappointed. Overall, the characters are thin, and there is no apparent depth in anything. In addition, the book is marked by a lot of violence in one place, and little violence in another, singling that the tone of the book is inconsistent throughout. I could not empathise with the plight of the characters, nor did I agree that people who are abandoned turn out weird; it sets a bad precedent. The author tried, but failed, to shock his readers with various hard core scenarios, and the feeling that I got was like seeing a bad B movie. It tries to be serious, but it is not. In total, the author appears to not have made his mind up with what he wanted this book to be, and though the idea behind the book was very promising, the end result was an unpalatable read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15449806379598117627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9784770015907" href="/book/show/1065864.Coin_Locker_Babies">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1255910796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17521008282060096856">For a long time I was anxious to read anything by Ryu Murakami. The Coin Locker Babies started off decent enough but later dragged. I kept wanting Coin Locker to reach the heights of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3439713.Kenzabur___e' title='KenzaburÅ Åe' rel='nofollow noopener'>KenzaburÅ Åe</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/35258.Yukio_Mishima' title='Yukio Mishima' rel='nofollow noopener'>Yukio Mishima</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3354.Haruki_Murakami' title='Haruki Murakami' rel='nofollow noopener'>Haruki Murakami</a>. It's a lot to ask considering these writers are legends of modern literature. But I'm selfish, I want the best.<br/><br/>Coin Locker's strong substance is diluted by too high a page count. There were stand-out scenes. It's unfortunate there was so much waiting in between. I'm </span>
  <span id="freeText17521008282060096856" style="display:none">For a long time I was anxious to read anything by Ryu Murakami. The Coin Locker Babies started off decent enough but later dragged. I kept wanting Coin Locker to reach the heights of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3439713.Kenzabur___e" title="KenzaburÅ Åe" rel="nofollow noopener">KenzaburÅ Åe</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/35258.Yukio_Mishima" title="Yukio Mishima" rel="nofollow noopener">Yukio Mishima</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3354.Haruki_Murakami" title="Haruki Murakami" rel="nofollow noopener">Haruki Murakami</a>. It's a lot to ask considering these writers are legends of modern literature. But I'm selfish, I want the best.<br /><br />Coin Locker's strong substance is diluted by too high a page count. There were stand-out scenes. It's unfortunate there was so much waiting in between. I'm still willing to give Murakami another chance.</span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_25365'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25365.Out"><img alt="Out" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1386749063l/25365._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UPzhqA1sRmJLYlQVknQpe9fEKaQSoLF70qh8jVjymGJwl+zXpVoFJtKTjn4dZM4uRjAI7Xg2mQ3wxycKLlIR6w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wRtwhiATwuwhWg/O5PZ2jN4/WuHzdtKqlfEAQWFnxWXhcH35iCWBqLir1aVr5pHZT8t7qJng+ty3nlvGF8dM7A==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer927710703095367765">RyÅ« <b>Murakami</b> (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/11015261._' rel='nofollow noopener'>æä¸ é¾</a>) is a Japanese novelist and filmmaker. He is not related to Haruki Murakami or Takashi Murakami.<br/><br/>Murakami's first work, the short novel Almost Transparent Blue, written while he was still a student, deals with promiscuity and drug use among disaffected Japanese youth. Critically acclaimed as a new style of literature, it won the newcomer's literature prize in 1976 despite some ob</span>
  <span id="freeText927710703095367765" style="display:none">RyÅ« <b>Murakami</b> (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/11015261._" rel="nofollow noopener">æä¸ é¾</a>) is a Japanese novelist and filmmaker. He is not related to Haruki Murakami or Takashi Murakami.<br /><br />Murakami's first work, the short novel Almost Transparent Blue, written while he was still a student, deals with promiscuity and drug use among disaffected Japanese youth. Critically acclaimed as a new style of literature, it won the newcomer's literature prize in 1976 despite some observers decrying it as decadent. Later the same year, Blue won the Akutagawa Prize, going on to become a best seller. In 1980, Murakami published the much longer novel Coin Locker Babies, again to critical acclaim.<br /><br />Takashi Miike's feature film Audition (1999) was based on one of his novels. Murakami reportedly liked it so much he gave Miike his blessing to adapt Coin Locker Babies. The screen play was worked on by director Jordan Galland. However, Miike could not raise funding for the project. An adaptation directed by Michele Civetta is currently in production.<br /><br />Murakami has played drums for a rock group called Coelacanth and hosted a TV talk show.</span>
  <a data-text-id="927710703095367765" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
